5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Security Audit: Missing Authentication Middleware in HTTP Handlers

## Your Task

Your security team is conducting an audit of the Grafana observability stack.
The pattern in `grafana/grafana` shows proper authentication middleware
usage: HTTP handlers are wrapped with `middleware.AuthenticateUser` to enforce
tenant authentication.

Your task is to **find Go source files in the Loki and Mimir repositories** that register HTTP handlers or routes **without applying
authentication middleware** such as `middleware.AuthenticateUser`.

For each file found, report:
- The repository (e.g., `sg-evals/grafana-loki`)
- The file path within the repository
- The specific endpoint path(s) registered without authentication

## Context

You are auditing a microservices observability stack. The `grafana/grafana`
repo correctly wraps its compactor deletion endpoint with authentication:

```go
// Example from pkg/compactor/ui.go — middleware applied correctly
mw := middleware.Merge(
    middleware.AuthenticateUser,
    deletion.TenantMiddleware(c.limits),
)
```

In contrast, some files in these repos may register endpoints directly
with `mux.HandleFunc(...)` without any auth middleware wrapping, or use
`RegisterRoute(...)` with `auth=false`. These are the files your audit needs
to surface.

## Available Resources

Your ecosystem includes the following repositories:
- `grafana/grafana` at v11.4.0
- `grafana/loki` at v3.3.4

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {
      "repo": "sg-evals/grafana-loki",
      "path": "relative/path/to/file.go",
      "endpoints": ["/endpoint/path/1", "/endpoint/path/2"]
    }
  ],
  "text": "Narrative citing specific repos, file paths, and endpoint paths registered without authentication."
}
```

**Important**: Use exact repo identifiers as they appear in Sourcegraph. The repos to audit are `sg-evals/grafana-loki` and `sg-evals/grafana-mimir`. Note: the `grafana/loki` repository corresponds to `sg-evals/grafana-loki` in Sourcegraph — use `sg-evals/grafana-loki` as the `repo` value in your answer. The oracle checks for `pkg/loki/modules.go` in `sg-evals/grafana-loki`.
**Note**: Sourcegraph MCP tools return repo names with a `github.com/` prefix (e.g., `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`). Strip this prefix in your answer — use `sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`, NOT `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`.

Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find the Go files that register handlers without authentication middleware?
- **Provenance**: Does your answer cite the specific repos and file paths?

\t// BloomStore is a dependency of IndexGateway and Bloom Planner & Builder.\n775: \t// Do not instantiate store and do not create a service if neither ar enabled.\n776: \tif !t.Cfg.BloomGateway.Enabled && !t.Cfg.BloomBuild.Enabled {\n777: \t\treturn nil, nil\n778: \t}\n779: \n780: \tif !config.UsingObjectStorageIndex(t.Cfg.SchemaConfig.Configs) {\n781: \t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"not using shipper index type\")\n782: \t}\n783: \n784: \tt.updateConfigForShipperStore()\n785: \n786: \tvar err error\n787: \tlogger := log.With(util_log.Logger, \"component\", \"bloomstore\")\n788: \n789: \treg := prometheus.DefaultRegisterer\n790: \tbsCfg := t.Cfg.StorageConfig.BloomShipperConfig\n791: \n792: \tvar metasCache cache.Cache\n793: \tif t.Cfg.isTarget(IndexGateway) && cache.IsCacheConfigured(bsCfg.MetasCache) {\n794: \t\tmetasCache, err = cache.New(bsCfg.MetasCache, reg, logger, stats.BloomMetasCache, constants.Loki)\n795: \n796: \t\t// always enable LRU cache\n797: \t\tlruCfg := bsCfg.MetasLRUCache\n798: \t\tlruCfg.Enabled = true\n799: \t\tlruCfg.PurgeInterval = 1 * time.Minute\n800: \t\tlruCache := cache.NewEmbeddedCache(\"inmemory-metas-lru\", lruCfg, reg, logger, stats.BloomMetasCache)\n801: \n802: \t\tmetasCache = cache.NewTiered([]cache.Cache{lruCache, metasCache})\n803: \t\tif err != nil {\n804: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create metas cache: %w\", err)\n805: \t\t}\n806: \t} else {\n807: \t\tlevel.Info(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"no metas cache configured\")\n808: \t}\n809: \n810: \tblocksCache := bloomshipper.NewFsBlocksCache(bsCfg.BlocksCache, reg, logger)\n811: \tif err = bloomshipper.LoadBlocksDirIntoCache(bsCfg.WorkingDirectory, blocksCache, logger); err != nil {\n812: \t\tlevel.Warn(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"failed to preload blocks cache\", \"err\", err)\n813: \t}\n814: \n815: \tvar pageAllocator mempool.Allocator\n816: \n817: \t// Set global BloomPageAllocator variable\n818: \tswitch bsCfg.MemoryManagement.BloomPageAllocationType {\n819: \tcase \"simple\":\n820: \t\tpageAllocator = &mempool.SimpleHeapAllocator{}\n821: \tcase 2)\n825: \tcase \"fixed\":\n826: \t\tpageAllocator = mempool.New(\"bloom-page-pool\", bsCfg.MemoryManagement.BloomPageMemPoolBuckets, reg)\n827: \tdefault:\n828: \t\t// should not happen as the type is validated upfront\n829: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create bloom store: invalid allocator type\")\n830: \t}\n831: \n832: \tt.BloomStore, err = nil\n841: }\n842: \n843: func (t *Loki) updateConfigForShipperStore() {\n844: \t// Always set these configs\n845: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Mode = t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n846: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Mode = t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n847: \n848: \tif t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode == indexgateway.RingMode {\n849: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Ring = t.indexGatewayRingManager.Ring\n850: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Ring = t.indexGatewayRingManager.Ring\n851: \t}\n852: \n853: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IngesterName = t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.ID\n854: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IngesterName = t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.ID\n855: \n856: \t// If RF > 1 and current or upcoming index type is boltdb-shipper then disable index dedupe and write dedupe cache.\n857: \t// This is to ensure that index entries are replicated to all the boltdb files in ingesters flushing replicated data.\n858: \tif t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.RingConfig.ReplicationFactor > 1 {\n859: \t\tt.Cfg.ChunkStoreConfig.DisableIndexDeduplication = true\n860: \t\tt.Cfg.ChunkStoreConfig.WriteDedupeCacheConfig = cache.Config{}\n861: \t}\n862: \n863: \tswitch true {\n864: \tcase t.Cfg.isTarget(Ingester), t.Cfg.isTarget(Write):\n865: \t\t// Use embedded cache for caching index in memory, this also significantly helps performance.\n866: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexQueriesCacheConfig = cache.Config{\n867: \t\t\tEmbeddedCache: cache.EmbeddedCacheConfig{\n868: \t\t\t\tEnabled:   true,\n869: \t\t\t\tMaxSizeMB: 200,\n870: \t\t\t\t// This is a small hack to save some CPU cycles.\n871: \t\t\t\t// We check if the object is still valid after pulling it from cache using the IndexCacheValidity value\n872: \t\t\t\t// however it has to be deserialized to do so, setting the cache validity to some arbitrary amount less than the\n873: \t\t\t\t// IndexCacheValidity guarantees the Embedded cache will expire the object first which can be done without\n874: \t\t\t\t// having to deserialize the object.\n875: \t\t\t\tTTL: t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity - 1*time.Minute,\n876: \t\t\t},\n877: \t\t}\n878: \n879: \t\t// We do not want ingester to unnecessarily keep downloading files\n880: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeWriteOnly\n881: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IngesterDBRetainPeriod = shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay(t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity, t.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.ResyncInterval)\n882: \n883: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeWriteOnly\n884: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IngesterDBRetainPeriod = shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay(t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity, t.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.ResyncInterval)\n885:
